### Post by chili555 on 2013-11-08
> driver=jmeWell, that's a new one on me! Please hook up the ethernet cable and try to connect. Then open a terminal and run and post:```
dmesg | grep -e jme -e eth0
nm-tool
```Fascinating.

lsmod
cat /etc/resolv.conf

### Post by praseodym on 2013-11-09
There are no nameservers in your /etc/resolv.conf:
```

echo -e "nameserver 8.8.8.8\nnameserver 8.8.4.4" | sudo tee -a /etc/resolv.conf
sudo service network-manager restart
```

---

### Post by praseodym on 2013-11-09
Remove all profiles in "cable" and "DSL" in the network-manager and reboot

### Post by chili555 on 2013-11-09
I saw this:> - Device: eth0 -----------------------------------------------------------------
Type: Wired
Driver: jme
State: unavailable
Default: no
HW Address: 00:90:F5:C1:F0:E0

Capabilities:
Carrier Detect: yes

Wired Properties
[COLOR="#FF0000"]Carrier: off[/COLOR]And I saw this: [http://superuser.com/questions/536748/plugged-in-network-cable-is-not-detected-possibly-related-to-green-ethernet](http://superuser.com/questions/536748/plugged-in-network-cable-is-not-detected-possibly-related-to-green-ethernet) Notice the same driver, jme and the same symptom, Link detected: no. Please try:```
sudo ethtool -s eth0 autoneg off speed 100 duplex full
```Now check:```
nm-tool
```Any changes? If it helps, we can explore the later driver as mentioned in the link. As it stands now, without ethernet *OR* wireless, it will be extremely challenging to download and install a new driver.

Nothing has changed, unfortunately.
Yesterday evening, i managed to get a wireless access, and I did update the jme driver, but again, no change. 
I also did another try, by changing the boot order in the bios, and setting the «boot from ethernet» option. But I get an error message saying that the connection was faulty, and to check the cable. The cable and the connection are fine, I'm currently using them from an other computer.
Therefore, it shows that the problem exist at very low level, may be it is a hardware failure (but every thing else works fine, and it is a laptop (=everything in the same motherboard), so it seems really strange). I even have visually check the quality of the soldering between the ethernet plug and the motherboard, but did not find any problem...
Anyway, thanks to anyone for your help.
